name:Sâ€uâ€sâ€uâ€sâ€uâ€sâ€uâ€sâ€uâ€mâ€aâ€lâ€i
info:Superior City-view Double Room
info:Stayed in August 2023
info:Solo travelers
info:36 Reviews
rating:2.7
posted:Posted August 18, 2023
msg:Let me talk about the advantages first, after all, there are not many:
The pool water is clean, the room is quite big, and the bedding is clean. The infrastructure is still at the old five-star level. The price is not high.
The following are all complaints:
Hotels really want to stay in new ones, not old ones. This hotel still has facilities, but the maintenance is very poor. It is indeed cheap for a reason. But to be honest, more than 400 a night is not very cheap in a small city, and I am really not satisfied with this level. The countertops in the room are warped, and there are stains on the sofa. The worst thing is that the air conditioner is buzzing and noisy, but it doesn't cool well. The room I was given at the beginning is facing east. There is probably an air conditioner outside or something below, which is very noisy. Add the sound of the air conditioner, it's simply terrible. After asking the front desk to change the room, the response was very timely, but the air conditioner in the new room is still noisy. I really don't have the energy to fix it, so I just live here. I am a person who doesn't sleep very lightly, and I just climbed the mountain, but I didn't sleep well. I used Ctrip's room upgrade rights, but the result was a so-called deluxe room in the corner. It is a bit big, but the room type is not decent at all. I would rather not upgrade if I knew it earlier.
The service is not standard enough, less than 4 stars, 3.5 level. No one in the lobby helped with the luggage. The front desk of the swimming pool is almost no service, and they didn't even know to provide hand cards. And there were no bath towels in the swimming pool. Fortunately, I brought a towel to wipe my hair, otherwise I don't know how to get out. There are no toiletries inside, and no slippers are provided. The floor mat hurts my feet. Why should my feet after climbing the mountain suffer this torture?
There is no convenient switch for the lights in the room. There is only a master control by the bed that can be turned off with one button. If you want to turn it on, there are two switches at the head of the bed, two in the bathroom, two next to the TV, and one in the hallway. You have to press all the switches. It's just too antique and tiring.
The seal of the shower room is not tight, and there is water all over the floor after taking a shower.
If I come to play next time, I'd better stay in a newer hotel...
----------------------------------------

name:Aâ€nâ€oâ€nâ€yâ€mâ€oâ€uâ€sâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Superior City-view Twin Room
info:Stayed in May 2023
info:Couples
info:16 Reviews
rating:4.5
posted:Posted May 31, 2023
msg:Baolong Yijun Hotel is about ten minutes' drive from the entrance of Mount Tai's Red Gate, and the Dai Temple Scenic Area is only about seven minutes away. The farthest Taohuayu is only 17 kilometers away. There are many specialties within a three-minute walk around the hotel. The hotel's Chinese restaurant also offers the best local Shandong cuisine. The buffet breakfast is rich in variety, the service is super good, and it feels like home. When we checked in on Monday, there were not many people, so we upgraded to a mountain view room for free. If the weather is good, you can sit in the room and watch the sunset. The hotel has two free parking lots on the ground and underground. It is recommended to park on the ground and enter the lobby conveniently. The underground parking lot is connected to the hotel restaurant. To get to the room, you need to go to the lobby first and then take another elevator to swipe the card to the room. Overall evaluation of the stay: Although the hotel facilities are a bit old, the room needs to bring its own plug to charge the mobile phone. But the highlight is that the staff has a special sense of team honor, attaches great importance to the guests' stay experience, and will actively solicit guests' opinions. As long as the problem is raised, whether it is the cleaning aunt, the buffet restaurant waiter, or the lobby duty manager, they will treat it as their own business and try their best to solve it, and it is very reassuring to live.
